mama ca mṛditaṃ kṣaumaṃ bālye tvadaṅgavivartanaiḥ 
anujanidhanasphītāc chokād atipraṇayāc ca yad
vacanavikṛtiṣv asya krodho mudhā kriyate tvayā SRs vesaṃ 
ity atra aśvatthāmaprārthanam anunayaḥ 
atha bhraṃśaḥ
patanaṃ prakṛtād arthād anyasmin bhraṃśa īritaḥ SRs b
yathā prasannarāghave
rāvaṇaḥ saṃvṛttanijarūpaḥ puruṣarūpeṇa praviṣṭaḥ 
kathaya kva tāvat karṇāntaniveśanīyaguṇaṃ kanyāratnaṃ kārmukaṃ ca 
mañjarīkaḥidaṃ tāvat kārmukam 
kanyā tu caramaṃ locanapatham avatariṣyati 
rāvaṇaḥ sasaṃrambham
dhiṅ mūrkha 
kathaṃ re rāśinakṣatrapāṭhakānāṃ goṣṭhīṃ na dṛṣṭavān asi 
te' pi kanyām eva prathamaṃ prakaṭayanti 
caramaṃ dhanuḥ 
mañjarīkaḥ svagatam
katham ayaṃ vācāṭatām eva prakaṭayati 
 padyād anantaram
ity atra rāvaṇena puruṣarūpeṇa praviṣṭena dhanuḥkanyayoḥ prakṛtam arthaṃ parityajya rāśilakṣaṇasyārthasya prasañjanād ayaṃ bhraṃśaḥ 
atha leśaḥ
leśaḥ syād iṅgitajñānakṛd viśeṣaṇavad vacaḥ SRs a
yathā mālatīmādhave kāmandakī
asau vidyāśābhiḥ śiśur api vinirgatya bhavanād
ihāyātaḥ sampraty avikalaśaraccandravadanaḥ 
yadālokasthāne bhavati puram unmādataralaiḥ
kaṭākṣair nārīṇāṃ kuvalayitavātāyanam iva SRs māmā 
ity atra kāmandakyā mālatyanurāgajñānanivedanasya unmādataralair iti viśeṣaṇasya kathanād ayaṃ leśaḥ 
atra kṣobhaḥ
kṣobhas tv anyagate hetāv anyasmin kāryakalpanaṃ SRs 
yathā ratnāvalyāṃ
rājā upasṛtya udbandhanam apanīyadevi 
kim idaṃ akāryaṃ kriyate 
mama kaṇṭhagatāḥ prāṇāḥ pāśe kaṇṭhagate tava 
anarthārthaprayatno' yaṃ tyajyatāṃ sāhasaṃ priye SRs ra 
atra pāśe vāsavadattākaṇṭhagate tatkāryabhūtasya prāṇānāṃ kaṇṭhagatatvasya vatsarājena svasmin kalpanāt kṣobhaḥ 
atha manorathaḥ
manorathas tu vyājena vivakṣitanivedanam SRs a
yathā śākuntale
śakuntalā padāntaraṃ gatvā parivṛtya prakāśam
ladāballaa saṃdābahāraa āmaṃtemi tumaṃ bhūobi pairbhoassa 
latāvalaya santāpahāraka āmantraye tvāṃ bhūyo' pi paribhogāya 
  padyād anantaram
atra latāmaṇḍapavyājena duṣyantāmantraṇaṃ manorathaḥ 
atha anuktasiddhiḥ
prastāvanaiva śeṣo' rtho yatrānukto' pi gṛhyate  
anuktasiddhir eṣā syād ity āha bharato muniḥ SRs
 Nāṭ   prastāvenaiva śeṣo' rthaḥ kṛtsno yan na pratīyate 
vacanena vinānuktasiddhiḥ sā parikīrtitā 
atha sārūpyaṃ
dṛṣṭaśrutānubhūtārthakathanādisamudbhavam  
sādṛśyaṃ yatra saṅkṣobhāt tat sārūpyaṃ nirūpyate SRs
yathā veṇisaṃhāre
praviśya gadāpāṇiḥ
bhīmaḥtiṣṭha tiṣṭha bhīru 
kvādhunā gamyate 
iti keśeṣu grahītum icchati
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ balād bhīmam āliṅgyadurātman 
bhīmārjunaśatro duryodhanahataka 
āśaiśavād anudinaṃ janitāparādhaḥ
kṣībo balena bhujayor hatarājaputra 
āsādya me' ntaram idaṃ bhujapañjarasaya
jīvan prayāsi na padāt padam adya pāpa SRs vesaṃ 
bhīmaḥaye katham āryaḥ suyodhanaśaṅkayā nirdayaṃ mām āliṅgati 
ity atra cārvākaśrāvitaduryodhanavijayasaṅkathāsaṅkṣepeṇa yudhiṣṭhirādīnāṃ bhīme suyodhanabuddhikathanād idaṃ sārūpyam 
atha mālā
īpsitārthaprasiddhyarthaṃ kathyante yatra sūribhiḥ  
prayojanāny anekāni sā mālety abhidhīyate SRs
yathā dhanañjayavijaye
gorakṣaṇaṃ samadaśātravamānabhaṅgaḥ
prītir virāṭanṛpater upakāriṇaś ca 
paryāptam ekam api me samartosavāya
sarvaṃ punar militam atra mamaiva bhāgyaiḥ SRs dhavi 
atha madhurabhāṣaṇam
yat prasannena manasā pūjyaṃ pūjayitur vacaḥ  
stutiprakāśanaṃ tat tu jñeyaṃ madhurabhāṣaṇam SRs
yathā anargharāghave
daśarathaḥ sapraśrayam
bhagavan viśvāmitra 
kaccit kāntārabhājāṃ bhavati paribhavaḥ ko' pi śauvāpado vā
pratyūhena kratūnāṃ na khalu makhabhujo bhuñjate vā havīṃṣi 
kartuṃ vā kaccid antar vasati vasumatīdakṣiṇaḥ saptatantur
yat samprāpto' si kiṃ vā raghukulatapasām īdṛśo' yaṃ vivartaḥ SRs arā 
viśvāmitraḥ vihasya
janayati tvayi vīra diśāṃ patīn
api gṛhāṅgaṇamātrakuṭumbinaḥ 
ripur iti śrutir eva na vāstavī
pratibhayonnatir astu kutas tu naḥ SRs arā 
ity ādāv anyonyaṃ pūjāvacanaṃ madhurabhāṣaṇam 
atha pṛcchā
praśnenaivottaraṃ yatra sā pṛcchā parikīrtitā SRs 
yathā
sarvakṣitibhṛtāṃ nātha dṛṣṭā sarvāṅgasundarī 
rāmā ramye vanānte' smin mayā virahitā tvayā SRs viu 
 ity atra parvatānāṃ nātha mayā virahitā priyā tvayā dṛṣṭeti praśne rājñāṃ nātha tvayā virahitā mayā dṛṣṭety uttarasya pratīyamānatvād iyaṃ 
atha upadiṣṭam
pratigṛhya tu śāstrārthaṃ yad vākyam abhidhīyate 
vidvanmanoharaṃ svantam upadiṣṭaṃ tad ucyate SRs 
yathā śākuntale
śakuntalā bhayaṃ nāṭayantī
paurava rakkha abiṇaaṃ 
maaṇasaṃtattābi ṇa hu attaṇo pahabāmi 
paurava rakṣa avinayam 
madanasantaptāpi na khalv ātmanaḥ prabhavāmi 
rājābhīru alaṃ gurujanād bhayena 
na te viditadharmā hi bhagavān doṣam atra grahīṣyati kulapatiḥ  api ca
gāndharveṇa vivāhena bahvyo rājarṣikanyakāḥ 
śrūyante pariṇītās tāḥ pitṛbhiś cānumoditāḥ SRs aśa 
ity atra śāstrānurodhenaiva pravṛttatvād idam upadiṣṭam 
atha dṛṣṭam
yathādeśaṃ yathākālaṃ yathārūpaṃ ca varṇyate 
yat pratyakṣaṃ parokṣaṃ vā tad dṛṣṭam dṛṣṭavan matam SRs 
yathā mālavikāgnimitre
rājāaho sarvāsv avasthāsu cārutā śobhāntaraṃ puṣyati  tathā hi
vāmaṃ sandhistimitavalayaṃ nyasya hastaṃ nitambe
kṛtvā śyāmāviṭapasadṛśaṃ srastamuktaṃ dvitīyam 
pādāṅguṣṭhālulitakusume kuṭṭime pātitākṣaṃ
nṛttād asyāḥ sthitam atitarāṃ kāntam ṛjvāyatārdham SRs māami 
ity atra itarasamakṣaṃ sthitāyāḥ saṃsthānajātivarṇanād idaṃ pratyakṣadṛṣṭam 
apratyakṣadṛṣṭaṃ
yathā padmāvatyāṃ
vyatyastapādakamalaṃ valitatribhaṅgī
saubhāgyam aṃsaviralīkṛtakeśapāśam 
piñchāvataṃsam urarīkṛtavaṃśanālaṃ
vyāmohanaṃ navam upaimi kṛpāviśeṣam SRs
ity atra apratyakṣasyaiva gopālasundarasya saṃsthānaviśeṣajātivarṇanād api dṛṣṭavad ābhāsanād idam apratyakṣadṛṣṭam 
śrīsiṃhabhūpena kavīśvarāṇāṃ
viśrāṇitānekavibhūṣaṇena 
ṣaṭtriṃśad uktāni hi bhūṣaṇāni
salakṣmalakṣyāṇi muner matena SRs 
sākṣad evopadeśena prāyo dharmasamanvayāt 
aṅgāṅgibhāvasampannasamastarasasaṃśrayāt SRs 
prakṛtyavasthāsandhyādisampattyupanibandhanāt 
āhuḥ prakaraṇādīnāṃ nāṭakaṃ prakṛtiṃ budhāḥ SRs 
atideśabalaprāpatanāṭakāṅgopajīvanāt 
anyāni rūpakāṇi syur vikārā nāṭakaṃ prati SRs 
ato hi lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvaṃ nāṭakasyābhidhīyate 
divyena vā mānuṣeṇa dhīrodāttena saṃyutam SRs 
śṛṅgāravīrānyatarapradhānarasasaṃśrayam 
khyāteti vṛttasambaddhaṃ sandhipañcakasaṃyutam SRs 
prakṛtyavasthāsandhyaṅgasandhyantaravibhūṣaṇaiḥ 
patākāsthānakair vṛttitadaṅgaiś ca pravṛttibhiḥ SRs 
viṣkambhakādibhir yuktaṃ nāṭakaṃ tat trivargadam 
tad etan nāṭakārambhaprakāro vakṣyate mayā SRs 
vidher yathaiva saṅkalpo mukhatāṃ pratipadyate 
pradhānasya prabandhasya tathā prastāvanā smṛtā SRs 
arthasya pratipādyasya tīrthaṃ prastāvanocyate 
prastāvanāyās tu mukhe nāndī kāryā śubhāvahā SRs 
āśīrnamaskriyāvastunirdeśānyatamā smṛtā 
candranāmāṅkitā prāyo maṅgalārthapadojjvalā SRs 
aṣṭābhir daśabhiś ceṣṭā seyaṃ dvādaśabhiḥ padaiḥ 
samair vā viṣamair vāpi prayojyety apare jaguḥ SRs 
tatrāśīranvitā nāndī yathābhirāmarāghave
kriyāsuḥ kalyāṇaṃ bhujagaśayanād utthitavataḥ
kaṭākṣāḥ kāruṇyapraṇayarasaveṇīlaharayaḥ 
harer lakṣmīlīlākamaladalasaubhāgyasuhṛdaḥ
sudhāsārasmerāḥ sucaritaviśeṣaikasulabhāḥ SRs
namaskriyāvatī nāndī
yathā uttararāmacarite
idaṃ kavibhyaḥ pūrvebhyah namovākaṃ praśāsmahe 
vandemahi ca tāṃ vāṇīm amṛtām ātmanaḥ kalām SRs urāca 
vastunirdeśavatī nāndī
yathā prabodhacandrodaye
antarnāḍīniyamitamarullaṅghitabrahmarandhraṃ
svānte śāntipraṇayini samunmīladānandasāndram 
pratyagjyotir jayati yaminaḥ spaṣṭalālāṭanetra
vyājavyaktīkṛtam iva jagadvyāpi candrārdhamauleḥ SRs praca 
aṣṭāpadānvitā
yathā mahāvīracarite
atha svasthāya devāya nityāya hatapāpmane 
tyaktakramavibhāgāya caitanyajyotiṣe namaḥ SRs mavīca 
daśapadānvitā yathā abhirāmarāghave kriyāsuḥ kalyāṇam ity ādi 
dvādaśapadānvitā
yathā anargharāghave
niṣpratyūham upāsmahe bhagavataḥ kaumodakīlakṣmaṇaḥ
kokaprīticakorapāraṇapaṭū jyotiṣmatī locane 
yābhyām ardhavibodhamugdhamadhuraśrīr ardhanidrāyito
nābhīpalvalapuṇḍarīkamukulaḥ kamboḥ sapatnīkṛtaḥ SRs arā 
atraiva maṅgalārthapadaprāyatvaṃ candranāmāṅkitatvaṃ ca draṣṭavyam 
nāndyante tu praviṣṭena sūtradhāreṇa dhīmatā 
prasādhanāya raṅgasya vṛttir yojyā hi bhāratī SRs 
aṅgāny asyāś ca catvāri bharatenāvabhāṣire 
prarocanāmukhe caiva vīthīprahasane iti SRs 
vīthī prahasanaṃ svasvaprasaṅge vakṣyate sphuṭam 
prarocanā tu sā proktā prakṛtārthapraśaṃsayā SRs 
sadasyacittavṛttīnāṃ saṃmukhīkaraṇaṃ ca yat 
praśaṃsā tu dvidhā jñeyā cetanācetanāśrayā  
acetanau deśakālau kālo madhuśaranmukhaḥ SRs
tatra vasantapraśaṃsayā prarocanā
yathā padmāvatyāṃ
rājatkorakakaṇṭakā madhukarījhaṅkārahuṅkāriṇīr
ālolastavakastanīr aviralādhūtapravālādharāḥ 
āliṅganti latāvadhūr atitarām āsannaśākhākarair
atyārūḍharasālasālarasikāḥ kānte vasantodaye SRs
śaratpraśaṃse
yathā veṇīsaṃhāre
satpakṣāṃ madhuragiraḥ prasādhitāśā madoddhatārambhāḥ 
nipatanti dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kālavaśān medinīpṛṣṭhe SRs vesaṃ 
atha deśaḥ
deśas tu devatārājatīrthasthānādir ucyate  
tad adya kālanāthasya yātretyādiṣu lakṣyatām SRs
cetanās tu kathānāthakavisabhyanaṭāḥ smṛtāḥ  
kathānāthās tu dharmārtharasamokṣopayoginaḥ SRs
dharmopayoginas tatra yudhiṣṭhiranalādayaḥ  
arthopayogino rudranarasiṃhanṛpādayaḥ SRs
rasopayogino vidyādharavatseśvarādayaḥ  
mokṣopayogino rāmavāsudevādayo matāḥ SRs
eke tv abhedam icchanti dharmamokṣopayoginoḥ SRs 
caturvidhāḥ kavayaḥ
kavayas tu prabandhāras te bhaveyuś caturvidhāḥ 
udātta uddhataḥ prauḍho vinīta iti bhedataḥ SRs 
tatra udāttaḥ
antargūḍhābhimānoktir udātta iti gīyate SRs a
yathā mālavikāgnimitre
purāṇam ity eva na sādhu sarvaṃ
na cāpi kāvyaṃ navam ity avadyam 
santaḥ parīkṣyāntarad bhajante
mūḍhaḥ parapratyayaneyabuddhiḥ SRs māami 
atra santaḥ parīkṣety anena svakṛteḥ parīkṣaṇakṣamatvakalpito nijagarvaḥ kālidāsena vivakṣita iti tasyodāttatvam 
atha uddhataḥ
parāpavādāt svotkarṣavādī tūddhata ucyate SRs 
yathā mālatīmādhave
ye nāma kecid iha naḥ prathayanty avajñāṃ
jānanti te kim api tān prati naiṣa yatnaḥ 
utpatsyate' sti mama ko' pi samānadharmā
kālo hy ayaṃ niravadhir vipulā ca pṛthvī SRs māmā 
atra jānanti te kim apīti parāpavādāt mama tu ko' pi samānadharmety ātmotkarṣakathanāc ca bhavabhūter uddhatatvam 
yathā prauḍhaḥ
yathocitanijotkarṣavādī prauḍha itīritaḥ SRs a
yathā karuṇākandale
kavir bhāradvājo jagadavadhijāgrannijayaśā
rasaśreṇīmarmavyavaharaṇahevākarasikaḥ 
yadīyānāṃ vācāṃ rasikahṛdayollāsanavidyāv
amandānandātmā pariṇamati sandarbhamahimā SRs
atra rasaprauḍhisandarbhaprasādayor nāṭakanirmāṇocitayor eva kathanāt nijotkarṣaṃ prakaṭayann ayaṃ kaviḥ prauḍha ity ucyate 
yuktyā nijotkarṣavādī prauḍha ity aparaiḥ smṛtaḥ SRs 
yathā mamaivanedānīntanadīpikā kim u tamaḥsaṅghātam unmūlayed ity ādi rasārṇavasudhākare  
 atra jyotsnādidṛṣṭāntamukhena mādhuryaujaḥprasādākhyānāṃ guṇānāṃ svasāhityaṃ rasaucityena sattāṃ pratipādayann ayaṃ kaviḥ prauḍha ity  
ucyate  
atha vinītaḥ
vinīto vinayotkarṣāt svāpakarṣaprakāśakaḥ SRs a
yathā rāmānande
guṇo na kaścin mama vāṅnibandhe
labhyeta yatnena gaveṣito' pi 
tathāpy amuṃ rāmakathāprabandhaṃ
santo' nurāgeṇa samādriyante SRs
atra vinayotkarṣād apakarṣam ātmany āropayann ayaṃ kavir vinīta ity ucyate 
atha sabhyāḥ
sabhyās tu vibudhair jñeyā ye didṛkṣānivtā janāḥ  
te' pi dvidhā prārthanīyāḥ prārthak iti ca sphuṭam SRs
idaṃ prayokṣye yuṣmābhir anujñā dīyatām iti  
samprārthyāḥ sūtradhāreṇa prārthanīyā iti smṛtāḥ SRs
tvayā prayogaḥ kriyatām ity utkaṇṭhitacetasaḥ  
ye sūtriṇaṃ prārthayante te sabhyāḥ prārthakāḥ smṛtāh SRs
atha naṭāḥ
raṅgopajīvinaḥ proktā naṭās te' pi tridhā smṛtāḥ  
vādakā gāyakāś caiva nartakāś ceti kovidaiḥ SRs
vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgādivādakā vādakāḥ smṛtāḥ  
ālāpanadhruvāgītagāyakā gāyakā matāḥ 
nānāprakārābhinayakartāro nartakāḥ smṛtāḥ SRs 
tad evam
vistarād uta saṅkṣepāt prayuñjīta prarocanām SRs a
tatra saṅkṣiptā prarocanā
yathā ratnāvalyām
śrīharṣo nipuṇaḥ kaviḥ pariṣad apy eṣā guṇagrāhiṇī
loke hāri ca vatsarājacaritaṃ nāṭye ca dakṣā vayam 
vastvekaikam apīha vāñchitaphalaprāpteḥ padaṃ kiṃ punar
madbhāgyopacayād ayaṃ samuditaḥ sarvo guṇānāṃ gaṇaḥ SRs ra 
atra kathānāyakakavisabhyanaṭānāṃ catūrṇāṃ saṅkṣepeṇa varṇanād iyaṃ saṅkṣiptaprarocanā 
vistarāt tu bālarāmāyaṇādiṣu draṣṭavyā 
evaṃ prarocayan sabhyān sūtrī kuryād athāmukham  
sūtradhāro naṭīṃ brūte svakāryaṃ prati yuktitaḥ SRs
prastutākṣepacitroktyā yat tad āmukham īritam  
trīṇyāmukhāṅgāny ucyante kathodghātaḥ pravartakaḥ SRs
prayogātiśayaś ceti teṣāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate  
sūtriṇo vākyam arthaṃ vā svetivṛttasamaṃ yadā 
svīkṛtya praviśet pātraṃ kathodghāto dvidhā mataḥ SRs 
tatra vākyena kathodghāto
yathā ratnāvalyāṃ
dvīpād anyasmād api madhyād api jalanidher diśo' py antāt 
ānīya jhaṭiti ghaṭayati vidhir abhimatam abhimukhībhūtaḥ SRs ra 
iti sūtradhārasya priyāsamāśvāsanavākyaṃ svasyānukūlatayā paṭhato yaugandharāyaṇasya praveśāt kathodghātaḥ 
arthena kathodghāto
yathā veṇīsaṃhāraḥ
nirvāṇavairadahanāḥ praśamādarīṇāṃ
nandantu pāṇḍutanayāḥ saha mādhavena 
raktaprasādhitabhuvaḥ kṣatavigrahāś ca
svasthā bhavantu kururājasutāḥ sabhṛtyāḥ SRs vesaṃ 
atrottarārdhe sūtradhāreṇa dhārtarāṣṭrāṇāṃ svargasthitinirupadravalakṣaṇayor arthayor
vivakṣitayoḥ satoḥ bhīmena svasthā bhavantu mayi jīvati dhārtarāṣṭrā iti nirupadravalakṣaṇasyaivārthaviśeṣasya
grahaṇena praveśaḥ kṛta iti ayam arthena kathodghātaḥ 
atha pravartakaḥ
ākṣiptaṃ kālasāmyena pravṛttiḥ syāt pravartakam SRs a
yathā bālarāmāyaṇe
prakaṭitarāmāmbhojaḥ kauśikavān sapadi lakṣmaṇānandī 
śaracāpanamanahetor ayam avatīrṇaḥ śaratsamayaḥ SRs bārā 
atra viśvāmitrarāmalakṣmaṇānāṃ śaratsamayavarṇanasāmyena praveśaḥ pravartakaḥ 
atha prayogātiśayaḥ 
eṣo' yam ity upakṣepāt sūtradhāraprayogataḥ  
prayogasūcanaṃ yatra prayogātiśayo hi saḥ SRs
yathā mālavikāgnimitre
śirasā prathamagṛhītām ājñām icchāmi pariṣadaḥ kartum 
devyā iva dhāriṇyāḥ sevādakṣaḥ parijano' yam SRs māami 
atrāyam ity upakṣepeṇākṣiptaḥ parijanapraveśaḥ prayogātiśayaḥ 
tathā ca śākuntale
tavāsmi gītarāgeṇa hāriṇā prasabhaṃ hṛtaḥ 
eṣa rājeva duṣyantaḥ sāraṅgeṇātiraṃhasā SRs aśā 
ity atra eṣa ity upakṣipto duṣyantapraveśaḥ prayogātiśayaḥ 
prastāvanāsthāpaneti dvidhā syād idam āmukham  
vidūṣakanaṭīpāripārśvikaiḥ saha saṃlāpan SRs
stokavīthyaṅgasahitāny āmukhāṅgāni sūtrabhṛt  
yojayed yatra nāṭyajñair eṣā prastāvanā smṛtā SRs
sarvāmukhāṅgavīthyaṅgasametair vākyavistaraiḥ  
sūtradhāro yatra naṭīvidūṣakanaṭādibhiḥ SRs
saṃlapana prastutaṃ cārtham ākṣipet sthāpanā hi sā  
śṛṅgārapracure nāṭye yogyaḥ syād āmukhakramaḥ SRs
ratnāvalydike prāyo lakṣyatāṃ kovidair ayam  
vīrādbhutādi prāye tu prāyaḥ prastāvanocitā SRs
anargharāghavādyeṣu prāyaśo vīkṣyatām iyam  
hāsyabībhatsaraudrādiprāye tu sthāpanā matā SRs
vīrabhadravijṛmbhādau sā prāyeṇa samīkṣyatām  
kathitāny āmukhāṅgāni vīthyaṅgāni pracakṣmahe SRs
āmukhe' pi ca vīthyāṃ ca sādhāraṇye' pi saṃmataḥ  
vīthyaṅgasaṃprathā teṣāṃ vīthyām āvaśyakatvataḥ SRs
udghātyakāvalagitaprapañcatrigate chalam  
vākkelyadhibale gaṇḍam avasyanditanālike SRs
asatpralāpavyāhārau mṛdavaṃ ca trayodaśa  
tatrodghātyakam anyonyālāpamālā dvidhā hi tat 
gūḍhārathapadaparyāyakramāt praśnottarakramāt SRs 
tatra gūḍhārthapadaparyāyakramād udghātyakaṃ
yathā vīrabhadravijṛmbhitanāmani ḍime
sakhe ko' yaṃ raudraḥ kathaya mahitaḥ ko' pi hi raso
raso nāmāyaṃ kaḥ smṛtisurabhir āsvādamahimā 
samāsvādaḥ ko' yaṃ kramagalitavedyāntaramatir
mano' vasthā jñātaṃ nanu vadasi nidrāntaram iti SRs
 atra raudrarasasvarūpavivecanāya rasāsvādāvasthālakṣaṇair gūḍhārthapadaparyāyair naṭasūtradhārayoḥ saṃlāpād idam ādimam udghātyakam 
praśnottarakramād
yathā tatraiva ḍime
sevyaṃ kiṃ param uttamasya caritaṃ lokottaraḥ kaḥ pumān
śrīsiṃhaḥ sa tu kīdṛśo vada nidhir dharmasya dharmas tu kaḥ 
satyoktir vacanaṃ tu kiṃ kavinutaṃ ko nāma tādṛk kavir
viśveśaḥ sa tu kīdṛśo vijayate viśveṣu viśveśavat SRs
atra gūḍhārthapadaparyāyarahitapraśnottarakrameṇa naṭasūtradhārayoḥ saṃlāpāt prakṛtakavivarṇanopayuktam idam udghātyakam 
atha avalagitam
dvidhāvalagitaṃ proktam arthāvalaganātmakam 
anyaprasaṅgād anyasya saṃsiddhiḥ prakṛtasya va SRs 
anyaprasaṅgād anyasya siddhyā avalagitaṃ
yathā abhirāmarāghave anapotanāyakīye
hanta sārasvataṃ cakṣuḥ kavīnāṃ krāntadarśinām 
atiśayya pravarteta niyatārtheṣu vastuṣu SRs
 atra sūtradhāreṇa kavīnāṃ sārasvataṃ cakṣur iti kavisāmānyavarṇanena svābhilaṣitakaviviśeṣotkarṣasādhanarūpāt prakṛtāerthāvalaganād avalagitam  
idam  
anyaprasaṅgena prakṛtasya siddhir
yathā anargharāghave
sūtradhāraḥmāriṣa
sthāne khalu bhavataḥ kutūhalam 
īdṛśam evaitat 
tat tādṛg ujjvalakakutsthakulapraśasti
saurabhyanirbharagabhīramanoharāṇi 
vālmīkivāgamṛtakūpanipānalakṣmīm
etāni bibhrati murārikaver vacāṃsi SRs arā 
atrāprakṛtavālmīkivarṇanaprasaṅgena prakṛtamāriṣakutūhalotkarṣasaṃsādhanarūpāt prakṛtanāṭyāvalaganād idaṃ dvitīyam avalagitam 
atha prapañcaḥ
prapañcas tu mithaḥ stotram asadbhūtaṃ ca hāsyakṛt SRs a
yathā vīrabhadravijṛmbhaṇe
nāṭyācāryas tvam asi suhṛdāṃ tvādṛśānāṃ prasādāt
ko' yaṃ gītaśramavidhir aho bhinnakaṇṭho' dya jātaḥ 
jñātaṃ jñātaṃ parihasasi māṃ bhāṣitair bhāvagarbhair
maivaṃ vācyaṃ tvam asi hi gurus tatra ceṣṭiḥ pramāṇam SRs
atra naṭasūtradhārayor anyathārthasyānyonyastotrasya hāsyāyaiva pravṛttatvāt prapañcaḥ 
atha trigatam
śrutisāmyād anekārthayojanaṃ trigataṃ bhavet SRs b
yathābhirāmarāghave
pāripārśvikaḥ
vāṇīmurajakvaṇitaṃ śrutisubhagaṃ kiṃ sudhāmucaḥ stanitam 
jaladasya kim ā jñātaṃ tava madhuragabhīravāgvilāso' yam SRs
atra sūtradhāravāgvilāse murajajaladadhvanivitarkasambhāvanāt trigatam 
atha chalam
proktaṃ chalaṃ sasotprāsaiḥ priyābhāsair vilobhanam SRs a
yathā abhirāmarāghave
vidvān asau kalāvān api rasiko bahuvidhaprayogajñaḥ 
iti ca bhavantaṃ vidmo nirvyūḍhaṃ sādhu tat tvayā sarvam SRs
atra viparītalakṣaṇayā prahelikārtham ajānataḥ pāripārśvikasyopālambhanāt chalam 
atha vākkeliḥ
sākāṅkṣasyaiva vākyasya vākkeliḥ syāt samāptitaḥ SRs 
yathā maheśvarānande
kulaśokaharaṃ kumāram ekaṃ
kuhanābhairavapāraṇonmukhābhyām 
upahūya kṛtādaraṃ pitṛbhyām
upari prastutam oṃ namaḥ śivāya SRs
atra vākye sākāṅkṣe viśeṣāṃśam anuktvā namaḥ śivāyeti samāptikathanād vākkeliḥ 
atha adhibalam
spardhayānyonyasāmarthyavyaktis tv adhibalaṃ bhavet SRs a
yathā vīrabhadravijṛmbhaṇe
mā bhūc cintā taveyaṃ mayi sati kuśale duṣkaraḥ kiṃ prayogo
mānin jānāsi kiṃ tvaṃ kim api na viditā cāturī me tvayā kim 
āstāṃ svastotrakanthā kṛtam iha kathaitair bhūtapūrvaiḥ prasaṅgaiḥ
patnyāhaṃ vaśyakarmā sapadi naṭavidhāv eṣa sajjībhavāmi SRs
atra naṭasūtradhārayoḥ parasparaspardhayā svasvaprayogasāmarthyaprakāśanād adhibalam 
atha gaṇḍam
gaṇḍaṃ prastutasambandhi bhinnārthaṃ sahasoditam SRs b
yathā veṇīsaṃhāre
nirvāṇavairadahanāḥ praśamādarīṇāṃ
nandantu pāṇḍutanayāḥ saha mādhavena 
raktaprasādhitabhuvaḥ kṣatavigrahāś ca
svasthā bhavantu kururājasutāḥ sabhṛtyāḥ  vesaṃ 
tatra sūtradhāreṇa nirupadravalakṣaṇe' rthe vivakṣite' pi svargasthitilakṣaṇārthasūcakasya
raktaprasādhitaabhuva ity ādiśliṣṭavākyasya sahasā prastutasambandhitayā bhāṣitatvād gaṇḍam 
atha avasyanditam
pūrvoktasyānyathā vyākhyā yatrāvasyanditaṃ hi tat SRs a
yathā veṇīsaṃhāre
sūtradhāraḥ
satpakṣā madhuragiraḥ prasādhitāśā madoddhatārambhāḥ 
nipatanti dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kālavaśān medinīpṛṣṭhe SRs vesaṃ 
pāripārśvikaḥ praviśya sambhrāntaḥ
śāntaṃ pāpam 
pratihatam amaṅgalam 
sūtradhāraḥmā bhaiṣīḥ 
nanu śaratsamayavarṇanāśaṃsayā haṃsān dhārtarāṣṭrā iti vyapadiśāmi 
atra pūrvoktasya suyodhanādinipātasya haṃsapātatvena vyākhyānād idam avasyanditam 
atha nālikā
prahelikā nigūḍhārthā hāsyārthaṃ nālikā smṛtā  
antarlāpā bahirlāpety eṣā dvedhā samīritā SRs
tatra antarlāpā
yathā prasannarāghave
pratyaṅkam aṅkuritasarvanavāvatāran
navyollasatkusumarājivirājibandham 
gharmetarāṃśum iva vakratayātiramyaṃ
nāṭyaprabandham atimañjulasaṃvidhānam SRs prarā 
atra prasannarāghavanāmety uttarasya saptākṣarāṣṭapaṅktikrameṇa likhite' sminn eva śloke mṛgyatvād antarlāpo nāmeyam 
bahirlāpā yathā bālarāmāyaṇe
kamabaḍḍhantavilāsaṃ rasāsale kaṃ karei kandappo 
kramavardhamānavilāsaṃ rasātale kaṃ karoti kandarpaḥ 
sūtradhāraḥaye praśnottaram 
seyam asmatprītir iti devādeśaḥ 
tat svayam eva vācayāmi
nirbhayagurur vyadhatta ca vālmīkikathāṃ kim anusṛtya SRs bārā 
ity atra bālarāmāyaṇam ity uttarasya bahir eva mṛgyatvād bahirlāpā nāma nālikeyam 
atha asatpralāpaḥ
asambaddhakathālāpo' satpralāpa itīritaḥ SRs b
yathā vīrabhadravijṛmbhaṇe naṭaḥ
patnī parilambikucā tanayā mama danturāpi taruṇavayāḥ 
krīḍākapir asti gṛhe tad ahaṃ nāṭyaprayogamarmajñaḥ SRs
atra naṭena svakīyanāṭyaprayogamarmajñatve hetutayā kathitānāṃ krīḍākapisadbhāvādīnām asambaddhatvād ayam asatpralāpaḥ 
atha vyāhāraḥ
anyārthaṃ vacanaṃ hāsyakaraṃ vyāhāra ucyate SRs a
yathā ānandakośanāmani prahasanepraviśya
naṭīayya ko ṇioo 
ārya ko niyogaḥ 
sūtradhāraḥārye gargarike nūnam ānandakośanābhilāṣiṇī pariṣad iyam 
naṭītā daṃsedu ayyo 
tado kiṃ bilaṃbeṇa 
tad darśayatu āryaḥ 
tataḥ kiṃ vilambena 
sūtradhāraḥayi gāyike gargarike bhavatyā mukhavyāpāreṇa bījotthāpanānusandhāyinā bhavitavyam 
naṭī saharṣam
kīriso so muhabābāro 
kīdṛśaḥ sa mukhyavyāpāraḥ 
sūtradhāraḥnanv amum eva śiśiram adhikṛtya dhruvāgānarūpaḥ 
ity atra ānandakośabījotthāpanamukhavyāpārāṇāṃ rūpakabījotthāpanadhruvāgānārthānām api anyārthapratītyā hāsyakaratvād ayaṃ vyāhāraḥ
atha mṛdavam
doṣā guṇā guṇā doṣā yatra syur mṛdavaṃ hi tat SRs b
yathā
nārhāḥ kevalavedapāṭhavidhinā kīrā iva chāndasāḥ
śāstrīyābhyasanāc chunām iva nṛṇām anyonyakolāhalaḥ 
vyarthaṃ kāvyam asatyavastughaṭanāt svapnendrajālādivad
vyākīrṇavyavahāranirṇayakṛte tv ekaiva kāryā smṛtiḥ SRs
atra kāvyādiṣu guṇabhūteṣv api doṣatvakathanād mṛdavam idam 
evam āmukham āyojya sūtradhāre sahānuge 
niṣkrānte' that tadākṣiptaiḥ pātrair vastu prapañcayet SRs 
vastu sarvaṃ dvidhā sūcyam asūcyam iti bhedataḥ 
rasahīnaṃ bhaved atra vastu tat sūcyam ucyate SRs 
yad vastu nīrasaṃ tat tu sūcayet sūcakās tv amī 
viṣkambhacūlikāṅkāsyāṅkāvatārapraveśakāḥ SRs 
tatra viṣkambho bhūtabhāvivastvaṃśasūcakaḥ 
amukhyapātraracitaḥ saṅkṣepaikaprayojanaḥ SRs 
sa śuddho miśra ity ukto miśraḥ syān nīcamadhyamaiḥ 
so' yaṃ ceṭīnaṭācāryasaṃlāpaparikalpitaḥ SRs 
mālavikāgnimitrasya prathamāṅke nirūpyatām 
śuddhaḥ kevalamadhyo' yam ekānekakṛto dvidhā SRs 
ratnāvalyām ekaśuddhaḥ prāptayaugandharāyaṇaḥ 
anekaśuddho viṣkambhaḥ ṣaṣṭhāṅke' nargharāghave  
nirūpyatāṃ samprayukto mālyavacchukasāraṇaiḥ SRs
atha cūlikā
vandimāgadhasūtādyaiḥ pratisīrāntarasthitaiḥ  
arthopakṣepaṇaṃ yat tu kriyate sā hi cūlikā SRs
sā dvidhā cūlikā khaṇḍacūlikā ceti bhedataḥ  
pātrair yavanikāntaḥsthaiḥ kevalaṃ yā tu nirmitā SRs
ādāv aṅkasya madhye vā cūlikā nāma sā smṛtā  
praveśanirgamābhāvād iyam aṅkād bahir gatā SRs
aṅkādau cūlikā
yathā anargharāghave saptamāṅke nepathye
tamisrāmūrcchālatrijagadagadṅkārakiraṇe
raghūṇāṃ gotrasya prasavitari deve savitari 
puraḥsthe dikpālaiḥ saha paragṛhāvāsavacanāt
praviṣṭo vaidehī dahanam atha śuddhā ca niragāt SRs arā 
ity ādau nepathyagatair eva pātraiḥ sītājvalanapraveśanirgamādīnām arthānāṃ prayogānucitānāṃ sūcanād iyaṃ cūlikā 
aṅkamadhye
yathā ratnāvalyāṃ dvitīyāṅke
nepathye kalakalaḥ
kaṇṭhe kṛttāvaśeṣaṃ kanakamayam adhaḥ śṛṅkhalādāma karṣan krāntvā dvārāṇi helācalacaraṇaraṇatkiṅkaṇīcakravālaḥ 
 dattātaṅko' ṅganānām anusṛtasaraṇiḥ sambhramād aśvapālaiḥ prabhraṣṭo' yaṃ plavaṅgaḥ praviśati nṛpater mandiraṃ mandurāyāḥ SRs ra 
atra nepathyagataiḥ pātraiḥ prayogānucitasya vānaraviplavādyarthasya sūcanād iyaṃ madhyacūlikā 
atha khaṇḍacūlikā
raṅganepathasaṃsthāyipātrasaṃlāpavistaraiḥ  
ādau kevalam aṅkasya kalpitā khaṇḍacūlikā 
praveśanirgamāprāpter iyam aṅkād bahirgatā SRs 
yathā bālarāmāyaṇe saptamāṅkasyādau
tataḥ praviśati vaitālikaḥ karpūracaṇḍaḥ
vaitālikaḥbhadra candanacaṇḍa parityaja nidrāmudrām 
vimuñca nijoṭajābhyantaram 
nepathyeayya kappuracaṃḍa esā miṭṭhā pabhādaṇiddā 
suvissaṃ dāva 
ārya karpūracaṇḍa eṣā miṣṭā prabhātanidrā 
svapsyāmi tāvat 
karpūracaṇḍaḥaho utsāhaśaktir bhavataḥ 
amantraśīlo mahīpatiḥ aparaprabandhadarśī kaviḥ apāṭharuciś ca vadnī na ciraṃ nandati 
nepathyetā ettha saṃttharatthido ṇimīlidaṇaaṇo jebba suppabhādaṃ paṭhissaṃ 
tad atra saṃstarasthito nimīlitanayana eva suprabhātaṃ paṭhiṣyāmi 
karpūracaṇḍaḥetad api bhavato bhūri 
tad upaślokayāvo rāmabhadram 
kiñcid uccaiḥ
mārtaṇḍaikakulaprakāṇḍatilakas trailokyarakṣāmaṇir
viśvāmitramahāmuner nirupadhiḥ śiṣyo raghugrāmaṇīḥ 
rāmas tāḍitatāṭakaḥ kim aparaṃ pratyakṣanārāyaṇaḥ
kausalyānayanotsavo vijayatāṃ bhūkāśyapasyātmajaḥ SRs bārā 
nepathye
kandappuddāmadappappasamaṇaguruṇo bahmaṇo kāladaṇḍe
pāṇiṃ deṃtassa gaṃgātaralidasasiṇo pabbaīballahassa 
cābaṃ caṃḍāhisiṃjārabaharidaṇahaṃ karṣaṇāruddhamajjhaṃ
jaṃ bhaggaṃ tassa saddo ṇisuṇiti huaṇe bittharaṃto ṇamāi SRs bārā 
kandarpoddāmadarpapraśamanaguror brahmaṇaḥ kāladaṇḍe
pāṇiṃ dātur gaṅgātaralitaśaśinaḥ parvatīvallabhasya 
cāpaṃ caṇḍābhiśiñjāravabharitanabhaḥ karṣaṇāruddhamadhyaṃ
yat bhagnaṃ tasya śabdo niḥśrūyate bhuvane vistaran na māti 
atra praviṣṭena karpūracaṇḍena yavanikāntargatena candanacaṇḍena ca paryāyapravṛttavāgvilāsais
tāṭakāvadhādivibhīṣaṇābhayapradānāntasya rāmabhadracaritasya bāhulyāt prayogānucitasya
sūcanād iyaṃ khaṇḍacūlikā 
enāṃ viṣkambham evānye prāhur naitan mataṃ mama 
apraviṣṭasya saṃlāpo viṣkambhe na hi yujyate  
tad viṣkambhaśiraskatvān mateyaṃ khaṇḍacūlikā SRs
atha aṅkāsyam
pūrvāṅkānte sampraviṣṭaiḥ pātrair bhāvyaṅkavastunaḥ  
sūcanaṃ tadavicchityai yat tad aṅkāsyam īritam SRs
yathā hi vīracarite dvitīyāṅkāvasānake  
praviṣṭena sumantreṇa sūcitaṃ rāmavigrahe SRs
vasiṣṭhaviśvāmitrādisamābhāṣaṇalakṣaṇam  
vastūttarāṅke pūrvārthāvicchedenaiva kalpitam SRs
athāṅkāvatāraḥ
aṅkāvatāraḥ pātrāṇāṃ pūrvakāryānuvartinām  
avibhāgena sarveṣāṃ bhāviny aṅke praveśanam SRs
dvitīyāṅke mālavikāgnimitre sa nirūpyatām  
pātreṇāṅkapraviṣṭena kevalaṃ sūcitatvataḥ 
bhaved aṅkād abāhyatvam aṅkāsyāṅkāvatārayoḥ SRs 
atha praveśakaḥ
yan nīcaiḥ kevalaṃ pātrair bhāvibhūtārthasūcanam 
aṅkayor ubhayor madhye sa vijñeyaḥ praveśakaḥ SRs 
so' yaṃ ceṭidvayālāpasaṃvidhānopakalpitaḥ 
mālatīmādhave prājñair dvitīyāṅke nirūpyatām SRs 
asūcyaṃ tu śubhodāttarasabhāvanirantaram 
prārambhe yady asūcyaṃ syād aṅkam evātra kalpayet SRs 
rasālaṅkāravastūnām upalālanakāṅkṣiṇām 
jananyaṅkavadādhārabhūtatvād aṅka ucyate SRs 
aṅkas tu pañcaṣair dvitrair aṅgino' ṅgasya vastunaḥ 
rasasya vā samālambabhūtaiḥ pātrair manoharaḥ  
saṃvidhānaviśeṣaḥ syāt tatrāsūcyaṃ prapañcayet SRs
atha asūcyavibhāgaḥ
asūcyaṃ tad dvidhā dṛśyaṃ śrāvyaṃ cādyaṃ tu darśayet  
dvedhā dvitīyaṃ svagataṃ prakāśaṃ ceti bhedataḥ SRs
svagataṃ svaikavijñeyaṃ prakāśaṃ tad dvidhā bhavet  
sarvaprakāśaṃ niyataprakāśaṃ ceti bhedataḥ SRs
sarvaprakāśaṃ sarveṣāṃ sthitānāṃ śravaṇocitam  
dvitīyaṃ tu sthiteṣv apy eṣv ekasya śravaṇocitam SRs
dvidhā vibhāvyate' nyac ca janāntam apavāritam  
tripatākākareṇānyān apavāryāntarā kathām SRs
anyenāmantraṇaṃ yat syāt taj janāntikam ucyate  
rahasyaṃ kathyate' nyasya parāvṛtyāpavāritam SRs
itthaṃ śrāvyaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ ca prayujya susamāhitaiḥ  
pātrair niṣkramaṇaṃ kāryam aṅkānte samam eva hi SRs
aṅkacchedaś ca kartavyaḥ kālāvasthānurodhataḥ  
dinārdhadinayor yogyam aṅke vastu pravartayet SRs
atha garbhāṅkaḥ
aṅkaprasaṅgād garbhāṅkalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣyate mayā  
rasanāyakavastūnāṃ mahotkarṣāya kovidaiḥ SRs
aṅkasya madhye yo' ṅkaḥ syād asau garbhāṅka īritaḥ  
vastusūcakanāndīko diṅmātramukhasaṅgataḥ SRs
arthopakṣepakair hīnaś cūlikāparivarjitaiḥ  
aneṣyadvastuviṣayaḥ pātraiś tricaturair yutaḥ SRs
nātiprapañcetivṛttaḥ svādhārāṅkāṅgaśobhitaḥ  
prastutārthānubandhī ca pātraniṣkramaṇāvadhiḥ SRs
prathamāṅke na kartavyaḥ so' yaṃ kāvyaviśāradaiḥ  
so' yam uttararāme tu rasotkarṣāya kathyatām SRs
netur utkarṣako jñeyo bālarāmāyaṇe tv ayam  
amogharāghave so' yaṃ vastūtkarṣaikakāraṇam SRs
nāṭake aṅkaniyamaḥ
nāṭake' ṅkā na kartavyāḥ pañcanyūnā daśādhikāḥ  
tad īdṛśaguṇopetaṃ nāṭakaṃ bhuktimuktidam SRs
tathā ca bharataḥ
dharmārthasādhanaṃ nāṭyaṃ sarvaduḥkhāpanodakṛt 
āsevadhvaṃ tad ṛṣayas tasyotthānaṃ tu nāṭakam SRs iti 
pūrṇādināṭakabhedānaṅgīkāraḥ
nāṭakasya tu pūrṇādibhedāḥ kecana kalpitāḥ  
teṣāṃ nātīva ramyatvād aparīkṣākṣamatvataḥ 
muninānādṛtatvāc ca tān uddeṣṭum udāsmahe SRs 
atha prakaraṇam
yatretivṛttam utpādyaṃ dhīraśāntaś ca nāyakaḥ 
rasaḥ pradhānaṃ śṛṅgāraḥ śeṣaṃ nāṭakavad bhavet SRs 
tad dhi prakaraṇaṃ śuddhaṃ dhūrtaṃ miśraṃ ca tat tridhā 
kulastrīnāyakaṃ śuddhaṃ mālatīmādhavādikam SRs 
gaṇikānāyikaṃ dhūrtaṃ kāmadattāhvayādikam 
kitavadhyputakārādivyāpāraṃ tv atra kalpayet SRs 
miśraṃ tat kulajāveśye kalpite yatra nāyike 
dhūrtaśuddhakramopetaṃ tan mṛcchakaṭikādikam SRs 
nāṭikāyāḥ na pṛthagrūpatvam
nāṭikā tv anayor bhedo na pṛthag rūpakaṃ bhavet 
prakhyātaṃ nṛpater vṛttaṃ nāṭakād āhṛtaṃ yataḥ SRs 
buddhikalpitavastutvaṃ tathā prakaraṇād api 
vimarśasandhirāhityaṃ bhedakaṃ cen na tan matam SRs 
ratnāvalyādike lakṣye tatsandher api darśanāt 
strīprāyacaturaṅkādibhedakaṃ cen na tan matam SRs 
ekadvitryaṅkapātrādibhedenānantatā yataḥ 
devīvaśāt saṅgamena bhedaś cet tan na yujyate 
mālavikāgnimitrādau nāṭikātvaprasaṅgataḥ SRs 
prakaraṇikānāṭikayor anusaraṇīyā hi nāṭikāsaraṇiḥ 
ata eva bharatamuninā nāṭyaṃ daśadhā nirūpitaṃ pūrvam SRs 
atha utṛṣṭikāṅkaḥ
khyātena vā kalpitena vastunā prākṛtair naraiḥ 
anvitaḥ kaiśikīhīnaḥ sāttvatyārabhaṭīmṛduḥ SRs 
strīṇāṃ vilāpavyāpārair upetaḥ karuṇāśrayaḥ 
nānāsaṅgrāmasaṃnāhaprahāramaraṇotkaṭaḥ SRs 
mukhanirvāhavān yaḥ syād ekadvitryaṅka icchayā 
utsṛṣṭikāṅkaḥ sa jñeyaḥ saviṣkambhapraveśakaḥ SRs 
asminn amaṅgalaprāye kuryān maṅgalam antataḥ 
prayojyasya vadhaḥ kāryaḥ punar ujjīvanāvadhiḥ SRs 
ujjīvanād apy adhikaṃ manorathaphalo' pi vā 
vijñeyam asya lakṣyaṃ tu karuṇākandalādikam SRs 
atha vyāyogaḥ
khātetivṛttasampanno niḥsahāyakanāyakaḥ 
yukto daśāvaraih khyātair uddhataiḥ pratināyakaiḥ SRs 
vimarśagarbharahito bhāratyārabhaṭīsphuṭaḥ 
hāsyaśṛṅgārarahita ekāṅko raudrasaṃśrayaḥ SRs 
ekavāsaravṛttāntaḥ prāptaviṣkambhacūlikaḥ 
astrīnimittasamaro vyāyogaḥ kathito budhaiḥ  
vijñeyam asya lakṣyaṃ tu dhanañjayajayādikam SRs
atha bhāṇaḥ
svasya vānyasya vā vṛttaṃ viṭena nipuṇoktinā  
śauryasaubhāgyasaṃstutyā vīraśṛṅgārasūcakam SRs
buddhikalpitam ekāṅkaṃ mukhanirvahaṇānvitam  
varṇyate bhāratīvṛttyā yatra taṃ bhāṇam īrate SRs
ekapātraprayojye' smin kuryād ākāśabhāṣitam  
anyenānuktam apy anyo vacaḥ śrutveva yad vadet SRs
iti kiṃ bhaṇasīty etad bhaved ākāśabhāṣitam  
lāsyāṅgāni daśaitasmin saṃyojyānyatra tāni tu SRs
geyapadaṃ sthitapāṭhyam āsīnaṃ puṣpagandhikā  
pracchedakas trimūḍhaṃ ca saindhavākhyaṃ dvimūḍhakam 
uttamottamakaṃ cānyad uktapratyuktam eva ca SRs 
atha geyapadam
vīṇādivādanenaiva sahitaṃ yatra bhāvyate 
lalitaṃ nāyikāgītaṃ tad geyapadam ucyate SRs 
cañcatpuṭādinā vākyābhinayo nāyikākṛtaḥ 
bhūmicārīpracāreṇa sthitapāṭhyaṃ tad ucyate SRs 
bhrūnetrapāṇicaraṇavilāsābhinayānvitam 
yojyam āsīnayā pāṭhyam āsīnaṃ tad udāhṛtam SRs 
nānāvidhena vādyena nānātālalayānvitam 
lāsyaṃ prayujyate yatra sā jñeyā puṣpagandhikā SRs 
anyāsaṅgamaśaṅkinyā nāyakasyātiroṣayā 
premacchedaprakaṭanaṃ lāsyaṃ pracchedakaṃ viduḥ SRs 
aniṣṭhuraślakṣṇapadaṃ samavṛttair alaṅkṛtam 
nāṭyaṃ puruṣabhāvāḍhyaṃ trimūḍhakam udāhṛtam SRs 
deśabhāṣāviśeṣeṇa caladvalayaśṛṅkhalam 
lāsyaṃ prayujyate yatra tat saindhavam iti smṛtam SRs 
cārībhir lalitābhiś ca citrārthābhinayānvitam 
spaṣṭabhāvarasopetaṃ lāsyaṃ yat tad dvimūḍhakam SRs 
aparijñātapārśvasthaṃ geyabhāvavibhūṣitam 
lāsyaṃ sotkaṇṭhavākyaṃ tad uttamottamakaṃ bhavet SRs 
kopaprasādajanitaṃ sādhikṣepapadāśrayam 
vākyaṃ tad uktapratyuktaṃ yūnoḥ praśnottarātmakam SRs 
śṛṅgāramañjarīmukhyam asyodāharaṇaṃ matam 
lāsyāṅgadaśakaṃ tatra lakṣyaṃ lakṣyavicakṣaṇaiḥ SRs 
atha samavakāraḥ
prakhyātenetivṛttena nāyakair api tadvidhaiḥ 
pṛthakprayojanāsaktair militair devadānavaiḥ SRs 
yuktaṃ dvādaśabhir vīrapradhānaṃ kaiśikīmṛdu 
tryaṅkaṃ vimarśahīnaṃ ca kapaṭatrayasaṃyutam SRs 
trividravaṃ triśṛṅgāraṃ vidyāt samavakārakam 
mohātmako bhramaḥ proktaḥ kapaṭas trividhas tv ayam SRs 
sattvajaḥ śatrujo daivajanitaś ceti sattvajaḥ 
krūraprāṇisamutpannaḥ śatrujas tu raṇādijaḥ SRs 
vātyāvarṣādisambhūto daivajaḥ kapaṭaḥ smṛtaḥ 
udāharaṇam eteṣām āvege lakṣyatāṃ budhaiḥ SRs 
jīvagrāho' pi moho vā kapaṭād vidravas tataḥ 
kapaṭatrayasambhūter ayaṃ ca trividho mataḥ  
dharmārthakāmasambaddhas tridhā śṛṅgāra īritaḥ SRs
dharmaśṛṅgāraḥ
vratādijanitaḥ kāmo dharmaśṛṅgāra īritaḥ  
pārvatīśivasambhogas tad udāharaṇaṃ matam SRs
arthaśṛṅgāraḥ
yatra kāmena sambaddhair arthair arthānubandhibhiḥ  
bhujyamānaiḥ sukhaprāptir arthaśṛṅgāra īritaḥ SRs
sārvabhaumaphalaprāptihetunā vatsabhūpateḥ  
ratnāvalyā samaṃ bhogo vijñeyā tad udāhṛtiḥ SRs
kāmaśṛṅgāraḥ
durādarasurāpānaparadārādikelijaḥ  
tattadāsvādalalitaḥ kāmaśṛṅgāra īritaḥ SRs
tad udāharaṇaṃ prāyo dṛśyaṃ prasanādiṣu  
śṛṅgāratritayaṃ tatra nātra bindupraveśakau SRs
mukhapratimukhe sandhī vastu dvādaśanāḍikam  
prathame kalpayed aṅke nāḍikā ghaṭikādvayam SRs
mukhādisandhitrayavāṃś caturnāḍikavastukaḥ  
dvitīyāṅkas tṛtīyas tu dvināḍikakathāśrayaḥ SRs
nirvimarśacatuḥsandhir evam aṅkās trayaḥ smṛtāḥ  
vīthīprahasanāṅgāni kuryād atra samāsataḥ SRs
prastāvanāyāḥ prastāve prokto vīthyaṅgavistaraḥ  
daśa prahasanāṅgāni tatprasaṅge pracakṣmahe 
udāharaṇam etasya payodhimathanādikam SRs 
atha vīthī
sūcyapradhānaśṛṅgārā mukhanirvahaṇānvitā 
ekayojyā dviyojyā vā kaiśikīvṛttinirmitā SRs 
vīthyaṅgasahitaikāṅkā vīthīti kathitā budhaiḥ 
asyāṃ prāyeṇa lāsyāṅgadaśakaṃ yojayen na vā SRs 
sāmānyā parakīyā vā nāyikātrānurāgiṇī 
vīthyaṅgaprāyavṛttitvān nocitā kulapālikā  
lakṣyam asyās tu vijñeyaṃ mādhavīvīthikādikam SRs
atha prahasanam
vastusandhyaṅkalāsyāṅgavṛttayo yatra bhāṇavat  
raso hāsyaḥ pradhānaṃ syād etat prahasanaṃ matam SRs
viśeṣeṇa daśāṅgāni kalpayed atra tāni tu  
avagalitāvaskandau vyavahāro vipralambha upapattiḥ 
bhayam anṛtaṃ vibhrāntir gadgadavāk ca pralāpaś ca SRs 
tatra avagalitam
pūrvam ātmagṛhītasya samācārasya mohataḥ 
dūṣaṇaṃ tyajanaṃ cātra dvidhāvagalitaṃ matam SRs 
yathā ānandakośanāmani prahasane
mithyātīrthaḥ
yāni dyanti galād adhaḥ sukṛtino lomnāṃ ca teṣāṃ sthitiṃ
yāny ūrdhvaṃ paripoṣayanti puruṣās teṣāṃ muhuḥ khaṇḍanam 
kṛtvā sarvajagadviruddhavidhinā sañcāriṇāṃ mādṛśāṃ
śrīgītā ca harītakī ca harato hantopabhogyaṃ vayaḥ SRs
atra kenāpi yatibhraṣṭena svagṛhītasya yatyāśramasya dūṣaṇād idam avagalitam 
tyajanād yathā prabodhacandrodaye
kṣapaṇakaḥ
ayi pīṇaghaṇatthaṇasohaṇi palitatthakulaṃgaviloaṇi 
jai lamasi kāvāliṇībhāvehiṃ sābakā kiṃ kalissaṃdi SRs
aho kāvāliṇīadaṃsaṇaṃ jebba ekkaṃ saukkhamokkhasāhaṇam 
prakāśam bho kābālia hagge tuhake saṃpadaṃ dāso saṃbutto 
maṃ pi mahābhairavānusāsaṇe dikkhaya 
ayi pīnaghanastanaśobhane paritrastakuraṅgavilocane 
yadi ramase kāpālinībhāvaiḥ śrāvakāḥ kiṃ kariṣyanti 
aho kāpālinīdarśanam eva ekaṃ saukhyamokṣasādhanam 
prakāśam bho kāpālika ahaṃ tava samprataṃ dāsaḥ saṃvṛttaḥ 
mām api mahābhairavānuśāsane dikṣaya 
ity ādau kṣapaṇakasya svamārgaparibhraṃśa avagalitam 
atha avaskandaḥ
avaskandas tv anekeṣām ayogyasyaikavastunaḥ 
sambandhābhāsakathanāt svasvayogyatvayojanā SRs 
yathā prahasane ānandakośanāmani
yatiḥsākṣād bhūtaṃ vadati kucayor antaraṃ dvaitavādaṃ
bauddhaḥdṛṣṭyor bhedaḥ kṣaṇikamahimā saugate dattapādaḥ 
jainaḥbāhvor mūle nayati śucitām arhatī kāpi dīkṣā
sarvenābher mūlaṃ prathayati phalaṃ sarvasiddhāntasāram SRs
atra yatibauddhajainānāṃ gaṇikāyāṃ svasvasiddhāntadharmasambandhakathanena svasvapakṣaparigrahayogyatvayojanād avaskandaḥ 
atha vyavahāraḥ
vyavahāras tu saṃvādo dvitrāṇāṃ hāsyakāraṇam SRs a
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
bauddhaḥ yatiṃ vilokya
kuto maṇḍa ekadaṇḍī 
mithyātīrthaḥ vilokya dṛṣṭim apakarṣan ātmagatam
kṣaṇikavādī na sambhāṣaṇīya eva 
tathāpi daṇḍam antardhāya niruttaraṃ karomi 
prakāśam aye śūnyavādin 
adaṇḍaḥ amuṇḍo' ham āgalād asmi 
jainaḥ ātmagatam
nūnam asau māyāvādī 
bhavatu 
aham api kim apy antardhāya prastutaṃ pṛcchāmi 
prakāśam aye mahāpariṇāmavādin 
bṛhadbīja lomnāṃ samānajātīyatve' pi keṣāñcit saṅkartanam anyeṣāṃ saṃrakṣaṇam iti vyavasthitau kiṃ pramāṇam 
mithyātīrthaḥjīvad amedhyaṃ jaṅgamanarako narapiśāco' yam antardhāyāpi na sambhāṣaṇīyaḥ 
niṣkacchakīrtiḥ sādaramsakhe 
ārhatamune vāde tvayā ayam apratipattiṃ nāma nigrahasthānam āropito māyāvādī 
mithyātīrthaḥ ātmagatam
nūnam imāv api mādṛśāv eva liṅgadhāraṇamātreṇa kukṣimbharaī syātām 
iti pippalamūlavedikāyāṃ niṣīdati 
ity atra yatibauddhajainānāṃ saṃvādo vyavahāraḥ 
atha vipralambhaḥ
vipralambho vañcanā syād bhūtāveśādikaitavāt SRs b
yathā prahasane ānandakośanāmani tatraiva
priyām ahaṃ pūrvabhṛtāṃ nāmnā svacchandabhakṣiṇī 
gṛhṇāmy enāṃ yadi trātuṃ kṛpā vaḥ śrūyatām idam SRs
surāghaṭānāṃ saptatyā viṃśatyā dṛptagaḍḍuraiḥ 
chāgaiś ca daśabhiḥ kāryā ciraṇṭītarpaṇakriyā SRs
adya kartum aśakyaṃ cet tatparyāptatamaṃ dhanam 
āsthāpyam asyāḥ sākṣiṇyāḥ jaraṭhāyāḥ paṭāñcale SRs
iti punar api vyāttavadanaṃ nṛtyati 
niṣkacchakīrtiḥhe vratinau 
kim atra vidheyam 
mithyātīrthaḥbhoḥ ahiṃsāvādin 
mriyamāṇaḥ prāṇī na rakṣaṇīya iti kiṃ yuṣmaddharmaḥ 
arūpāmbaraḥ sākṣepam
ekena sukham upādeyam 
anyena dhanaṃ pradeyam iti kiṃ yuṣmaddharmaḥ 
niṣkacchakīrtiḥ sāntarhāsaṃ svadhanaṃ yatidhanaṃ ca jaraṭhāyāḥ paṭāñcale baddhvā sabalātkāraṃ jainasya kaṭakaṃ tasyāḥ pādamūle' rpayati
madhumallikā sāṅgabhaṅgaṃ sasmraṇabhayam iva
ammo devadā vilambeṇa kuppissadi 
tā ciraṃṭiātappaṇaṃ kāduṃ gacchemi 
amho 
devatā vilambena kopiṣyati 
tat ciraṇṭikātarpaṇaṃ kartuṃ gacchāmi 
 iti kaṭakam ādāya niṣkrāntā 
ity ādau bhūtāveśakaitavena jainabauddhasaṃnyāsino vilobhya dhanaṃ kayāpi gaṇikayā gṛhītam ity ayaṃ vipralambhaḥ 
atha upapattiḥ
upapattis tu sā proktā yat prasiddhasya vastunaḥ 
lokaprasiddhayā yuktyā sādhanaṃ hāsyahetunā SRs 
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
mithyātīrthaḥ puro' valokya
aye upasarittīre pippalanāmā vanaspatiḥ 
yaś ca gītāsu bhagavatā nijavibhūtitayā nirdiṣṭaḥ 
vicintya katham asya taror iyatī mahimasambhāvanā 
vimṛśya upapadyata eva
tat padaṃ tanumadhyāyā yenāśvatthadalopamam 
tadaśvattho' smi vṛkṣāṇām ity ūce bhagavān hariḥ SRs iti 
 atra lokaprasiddhena aśvatthadalorumūlayoḥ sāmyena hetunā lokaprasiddhasyaiva bhagavadaśvatthayor aikyasya sādhanaṃ hāsyakāraṇam upapattiḥ 
atha bhayam
smṛtaṃ bhayaṃ tu nagaraśodhakādikṛto daraḥ SRs a
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
jainaḥaho arājako' yaṃ viṣayaḥ yat nagaraparisarāśritatapasvināṃ dhanaṃ coryate ity udvāhur ākrośati 
nagararakṣakāḥaye kim apahṛtaṃ dhanam 
kiyat iti taṃ paritaḥ praviśya parisarpanti 
arūpāmbaraḥdhik kaṣṭam 
nagaraśīghrakāḥ samāyānti 
ity ūrdhvabāhur oṣṭhaspandanaṃ karoti 
mithyātīrtho gaṇikām ākṣipya samādhiṃ nāṭayati 
niṣkacchakīrtir ekapādenāvatiṣṭhamānaḥ karāṅgulīr gaṇayati
ity ādau jainādīnāṃ bhayakathanād bhayam 
atha anṛtam
anṛtaṃ tu bhaved vākyam asabhyastutigumphitam  
tad evānṛtam ity āhur apare svamatastuteḥ SRs
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
bālātapena parimṛṣṭam ivāravindaṃ
māñjiṣṭhacelam iva mānmatham ātapatram 
sālaktalekham iva saukhyakaraṇḍam adya
yūnāṃ mude taruṇi tat padam ārtavaṃ te SRs
atra ārtavāruṇasyorumūlasya asabhyasya
varṇanād idam anṛtam 
aparaṃ yathā karpūramañjaryām
bhairavānandaḥ
raṃḍā caṃḍā dikkhadā dhammadārā
majjaṃ maṃsaṃ pijjae khajjae a 
bhikkhā bhojjaṃ cammakhaṇḍaṃ ca sejjā
kolo dhammo kassa ṇo bhādi rammo SRs kamaṃ 
raṇḍā caṇḍā dīkṣitā dharmadārā
madyaṃ māṃsaṃ pīyate khādyate ca 
bhikṣā bhojyaṃ carmakhaṇḍaṃ ca śayyā
kaulo dharmaḥ kasya no bhāti ramyaḥ 
atha vibhrāntiḥ
vastusāmyakṛto moho vibhrāntir iti gīyate SRs b
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
bauddhaḥ puro' valokya
hemakumbhavatī ramyatoraṇā cārudarpaṇā 
kāpi gandharvanagarī dṛśyate bhūmicāriṇī SRs
jainaḥaye kṣaṇabhaṅgavādin etad utpātaphalaṃ prathamadarśino bhavata eva pariṇamet 
iti locane nimīlayati 
bauddhaḥ punar nirvarṇya
hanta kim apade bhrānto' smi 
na purīyaṃ viśālākṣī na toraṇam ime bhruvau 
na darpaṇam imau gaṇḍau na ca kumbhāv imau stanau SRs
ity atra bauddhasya moho vibhrāntiḥ 
atha gadgadavāk
asatyaruditonmiśraṃ vākyaṃ gadgadavāg bhavet SRs a
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
bhaginyau parasparam āśliṣya rudita iva
guhyagrāhī ātmagatam
anupāttabāṣpakaṇikaṃ gadgadaniḥśvāsakalitam avyaktam 
anayor asatyaruditaṃ suratāntadaśāṃ vyanaktīva SRs
atra gadgadavāktvaṃ spaṣṭam 
atha pralāpaḥ
pralāpaḥ syād ayogyasya yogyatvenānumodanam SRs b
yathā tatraiva prahasane ānandakośanāmani
rājā saudāryodrekam
aye viḍālākṣa asmadīye nagare viṣaye ca
patihīnā ca yā nārī jāyāhīnaś ca yaḥ pumān 
tau dampatī yathākāmaṃ bhavetām iti ghuṣyatām SRs
viḍālākṣaḥdevaḥ pramāṇam 
iti sānucaro niṣkrāntaḥ 
guhyagrāhī saślāghāgauravam
naṣṭāśvabhagnaśakaṭanyāyena pratipāditam 
ucitā te mahārāja seyaṃ kāruṇyaghoṣaṇā SRs
api ca
manvādayo mahīpālāḥ śataśo gām apālayan 
na kenāpi kṛto mārga evam āścaryaśaukhyadaḥ SRs
atra ayogyasyāpi rājādeśasya dharmādhikāriṇā guhyagrāhiṇā nyāyaparikalpanayā yogyatvenānumodanād ayaṃ pralāpaḥ 
prahasanasya śuddhādibhedāḥ
śuddhaṃ kīrṇaṃ vaikṛtaṃ ca tac ca prahasanaṃ tridhā 
śuddhaṃ śrotriyaśākhāder veṣabhāṣādisaṃyutam SRs 
ceṭaceṭījanavyāptaṃ tal lakṣyaṃ tu nirūpyatām 
ānandakośapramukhaṃ tathā bhagavadajjukam SRs 
kīrṇaṃ tu sarvair vīthyaṅgaiḥ saṅkīrṇaṃ dhūrtasaṅkulam 
tasyodāharaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ bṛhatsaubhadrakādikam SRs 
yac cedaṃ kāmukādīnāṃ veṣabhāṣādisaṅgataiḥ 
ṣaṇḍatāpasavṛddhādyair yutaṃ tad vaikṛtaṃ bhavet  
kalikeliprahasanapramukhaṃ tad udāhṛtam SRs
atha ḍimaḥ
khyātetivṛttaṃ nirhāsyaśṛṅgāraṃ raudramudritam  
sāttvatīvṛttiviralaṃ bhāratyārabhaṭīsphuṭam SRs
nāyakair uddhatair devayakṣarākṣasapannagaiḥ  
gandharvabhūtavetālasiddhavidyādharādibhiḥ SRs
samanvitaṃ ṣoḍaśabhir nyāyamārgaṇanāyakam  
caturbhir āṅkair anvītaṃ nirvimarśakasandhibhiḥ SRs
nirghātolkoparāgādighorakrūrājisambhramam  
sapraveśakaviṣkambhacūlikaṃ hi ḍimaṃ viduḥ 
asyodāharaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ vīrabhadravijṛmbhitam SRs 
atha īhāmṛgaḥ
yatretivṛttaṃ miśraṃ syāt saviṣkambhapraveśakam 
catvāro' ṅkā nirvimarśagarbhāḥ syuḥ sandhayas trayaḥ SRs 
dhīroddhattaś ca prakhyāto divyo martyo' pi nāyakaḥ 
divyastriyam anicchantīṃ kanyāṃ vāhartum udyataḥ SRs 
strīnimittājisaṃrambhaḥ pañcaṣāḥ pratināyakāḥ 
rasā nirbhayabībhatsā vṛttayaḥ kaiśikīṃ vinā SRs 
svalpas tasyāḥ praveśo vā so' yam īhāmṛgo mataḥ 
vyājān nivārayed atra saṅgrāmaṃ bhīṣaṇakramam SRs 
tasyodāharaṇaṃ jñeyaṃ prājñair māyākuraṅgikā 
itthaṃ śrīsiṃhabhūpena sarvalakṣaṇaśālinā  
sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇo lakṣito rūpakakramaḥ SRs
atha nāṭakaparibhāṣā
atha rūpakanirmāṇaparijñānopayoginī  
śrīsiṃhadharaṇīśena paribhāṣā nirūpyate SRs
paribhāṣātra maryādā pūrvācāryopakalpitā  
sā hi naur atigambhīraṃ vivikṣor nāṭyasāgaram SRs
eṣā ca bhāṣānirdeśanāmabhis trividhā matā  
tatra bhāṣā dvidhā bhāṣā vibhāṣā ceti bhedataḥ SRs
caturdaśa vibhāṣāḥ syuḥ prācyādyā vākyavṛttayaḥ  
āsāṃ saṃskārarāhityād viniyogo na kathyate SRs
uttamādiṣu taddeśavyavahārāt pratīyatām  
bhāṣā dvidhā saṃskṛtā ca prākṛtī ceti bhedataḥ SRs
kaumārapāṇinīyādisaṃskṛtā saṃskṛtā matā  
iyaṃ tu devatādīnāṃ munīnāṃ nāyakasya ca 
liṅgināṃ ca viṭādīnm anīcānāṃ prayujyate SRs 
atha prākṛtī
prakṛteḥ saṃskṛtāyās tu vikṛtiḥ prākṛtī matā  
ṣaḍvidhā sā prākṛtaṃ ca śaurasenī ca māgadhī SRs
paiśācī cūlikā paiśācy apabhraṃśa iti kramāt  
atra tu prākṛtaṃ strīṇāṃ sarvāsāṃ niyataṃ bhavet SRs
kvacic ca devī gaṇikā mantrijā ceti yoṣitām  
yoginyapsarasoḥ śilpakāriṇyā api saṃskṛtam SRs
ye nīcāḥ karmaṇā jātyā teṣāṃ prākṛtam ucyate  
chadmaliṅgavatāṃ tadvaj jainānām iti kecana SRs
adhame madhyame cāpi śaurasenī prayujyate  
dhīvarādyatinīceṣu māgadhī ca niyujyate SRs
rakṣaḥpiśācanīceṣu paiśācīdvitayaṃ bhavet  
apabhraṃśas tu caṇḍālayavanādiṣu yujyate SRs
nāṭakādāv apabhraṃśavinyāsasyāsahiṣṇavaḥ  
anye caṇḍālakādīnāṃ māgadhyādīn prayuñjate SRs
sarveṣāṃ kāraṇavaśāt kāryo bhāṣāvyatikramaḥ  
māhātmyasya paribhraṃśaṃ madasyātiśayaṃ tathā SRs
pracchādanaṃ ca vibhrāntiṃ yathālikhitavācanam  
kadācid anuvādaṃ ca kāraṇāni pracakṣate SRs
atha nirdeśaparibhāṣā
sākṣād anāmagrāhyāṇāṃ janānāṃ pratisaṃjñayā  
āhvānabhaṅgī nāṭyajñair nirdeśa iti gīyate SRs
sa tridhā pūjyasadṛśakaniṣṭhaviṣayatvataḥ  
pūjyās tu devo munayo liṅginas tatsamāstriyaḥ SRs
bahuśrutāś ca bhagavacchabdavācyā bhavanti hi  
āryeti brāhmaṇo vācyo vṛddhas tāteti bhāṣyate SRs
upādhyāyeti cācāryo gaṇikā tv ajjukākhyayā  
mahārājeti bhūpālo vidvān bhāva itīryate SRs
chandato nāmabhir vācyā brāhmaṇais tu narādhipāḥ  
deveti nṛpatir vācyo bhṛtyaiḥ prakṛtibhis tathā SRs
sārvabhaumaḥ parijanair bhaṭṭabhaṭṭāraketi ca  
vācyo rājeti munibhir apatyapratyayena vā SRs
vidūṣakeṇa tu prāyaḥ sakhe rājan nitīcchayā  
brāhmaṇaiḥ sacivo vācyo hy amātya saciveti ca SRs
śaiṣāir āryety athāyuṣman iti sārathinā rathī  
tapasvisādhuśabdābhyāṃ praśāntaḥ paribhāṣyate SRs
svāmīti yuvarājas tu kumāro bhartṛdārakaḥ  
āvutteti svasur bhartā syāleti pṛtanāpatiḥ SRs
bhaṭṭinī svāminī devī tathā bhaṭṭāriketi ca  
paricārajanair vācyā yoṣito rājavallabhāḥ SRs
rājñā tu mahiṣī vācyā devīty anyāḥ priyā iti  
sarveṇa patnī tv āryeti pitur nāmnā sutasya vā SRs
tātapādā iti pitā mātāmbeti sutena tu  
jyeṣṭhās tv āryā iti bhrātrā tathā syur mātulādayaḥ SRs
atha sadṛśanirdeśaḥ
sadṛśaḥ sadṛśo vācyo vayasyety āhvayena vā  
haleti sakhyā tu sakhī kathanīyā sakhīti vā SRs
atha kaniṣṭhanirdeśaḥ
sutaśiṣyakanīyāṃso vācyā gurujanena hi  
vatsaputrakadīrghāyustātajāteti saṃjñayā SRs
anyaḥ kanīyān āryeṇa janena paribhāṣyate  
śilpādhikāranāmabhyāṃ bhadra bhadramukheti SRs
vācye nīcātinīce tu haṇḍe hañje iti kramāt  
bhartrā vācyāḥ svasvanāmnā bhṛtyāḥ śilpocitena vā SRs
evam ādi prakāreṇa yojyā nirdeśayojanā  
lokaśāstrāvirodhena vijñeyā kāvyakovidaiḥ SRs
atha nāmaparibhāṣā
anuktanāmnaḥ prakhyāte kañcukiprabhṛter api  
itivṛtte kalpite tu nāyakāder api sphuṭam SRs
rasavastūpayogīni kavir nāmāni kalpayet  
vinayandharabābhravyajayandharajayādikam SRs
kāryaṃ kañcukināṃ nāma prāyo viśvāsasūcakam  
latālaṅkārapuṣpādivastūnāṃ lalitātmanām SRs
nāmabhir guṇasiddhair ceṭīnāṃ nāma kalpayet  
karabhaḥ kalahaṃsaś cety ādi nāmānujīvinām SRs
karpūracaṇḍakāmpilyety ādikaṃ nāma vandinām  
subuddhivasubhūtyādimantriṇāṃ nāma kalpayet SRs
devarātaḥ somarāta iti nāma purodhasaḥ  
śrīvatso gautamaḥ kautso gārgyo maudgalya ity api SRs
vasantakaḥ kāpileya ity ākhyeyo vidūṣakaḥ  
pratāpavīravijayamānavikramasāhasaiḥ SRs
vasantabhūṣaṇottaṃsaśekharāṅkapadottaraiḥ  
dhīrottarāṇāṃ netṝṇāṃ nāma kurvīta kovidaḥ SRs
candrāpīḍaḥ kāmapāla ity ādyaṃ lalitātmanām  
ugravarmā caṇḍasena ity ādyuddhatacetasām SRs
dattasenāntanāmāni vaiśyānāṃ kalpayet sudhīḥ  
karpūramañjarī candralekhā rāgataraṅgikā SRs
padmāvatīti prāyeṇa nāmnā vācyā hi nāyikā  
devyas tu dhāriṇīlakṣmīvasumatyādināmabhiḥ SRs
bhogavatī kāntimatī kamalā kāmavallarī  
irāvatī haṃsapadīty ādināmnā tu bhoginī SRs
viprakṣatraviśaḥ śarmavarmadattāntanāmabhiḥ  
śikhaṇḍāṅgadacūḍāntanāmnā vidyādharādhipāḥ SRs
kuṇḍalānandaghaṇṭāntanāmnā kāpālikā janāḥ  
yogasundarikā vaṃśaprabhā vikaṭamudrikā SRs
śaṅkhakeyūrikety ādināmnā kāpālikastriyaḥ  
ānandinī siddhimatī śrīmatī sarvamaṅgalā SRs
yaśovatī putravatīty ādināmnā suvāsinī  
ity ādi sarvam ālocya lakṣaṇaṃ kṛtabuddhinā SRs
kavinā kalpitaṃ kāvyam ācandrārkaṃ prakāśate  
lakṣyalakṣaṇanirmāṇavijñānakṛtabuddhibhiḥ SRs
parīkṣyatām ayaṃ grantho vimatsaramanīṣayā  
bharatāgamapārīṇaḥ śrīmān siṃhamahīpatiḥ 
rasikaḥ kṛtavān evaṃ rasārṇavasudhākaram SRs 
saṃrambhād anapotasiṃhanṛpater dhāṭīsamāṭīkane
niḥsāṇeṣu dhaṇaṃ dhaṇaṃ dhaṇam iti dhvānānusandhāyiṣu 
modante hi raṇaṃ raṇaṃ raṇam iti prauḍhās tadīyā bhaṭā
bhrāntiṃ yānti tṛṇaṃ tṛṇaṃ tṛṇam iti pratyarthipṛthvībhujaḥ SRs 
matvā dhātrā tulāyāṃ laghur iti dharaṇīṃ siṃhabhūpālacandre
sṛṣṭe tatrātigurvyāṃ tadupanidhitayā sthāpyamānaiḥ krameṇa 
cintāratnaughakalpadrumatatisurabhīmaṇḍalaiḥ pūritāntāpy
ūrdhvaṃ nītā laghimnā tadarikulaśataiḥ pūryate' dyāpi sā dyauḥ SRs 
iti śrīmadāndhramaṇḍalādhīśvarapratigaṇḍabhairavaśrīmadanapotanarendranandanabhujabalabhīmaśrīsiṃhabhūpālaviracite
rasārṇavasudhākaranāmni nāṭyālaṅkāraśāstre bhāvakollāso nāma
tṛtīyo vilāsaḥ 
samāptaś cāyaṃ rasārṇavasudhākaraḥ
śrītoyaśailavasatiḥ sa tamālanīlo
jīyād dharir municakorasuśāradenduḥ 
lakṣmīstanastavakakuṅkumakardamaśrī
saṃliptanirmalaviśālabhujāntarālaḥ 
malayagirinivāsī māruto yacchatāṅgas
taruṇaśiśiraraśmir yat suhṛtpuṇyakīrtiḥ 
carati ciram anaṅgaḥ kvāpi kari apy adṛśyaḥ
sa jayatu rasikaughair vanditaḥ pañcabāṇaḥ 
aśeṣāṇāṃ dvijanuṣām āśīrvādaparamparā 
taraṅgayatu kalyāṇaṃ kavīnāṃ cāyur āyatam
